[2024-03-03, 5:06:24 PM] Sass Khazzam: Years ago I used to do the big Sunday NYT every week. It would be published in the Saturday Montreal Gazette 6 days later. 

It used to take me up to a week to do it. I did it in pencil at the beginning, but as I got better, I began to do it in ink. 

However, I never did it with a timer! This notion went against the grain of solving the puzzle.

Initially, the difficult parts would get rather messy. But as I got better, I only inked in what I was sure of, until the puzzle would start to take some shape and I could be more certain of my choices.
I got to the point where I could once in a while do the puzzle in an afternoon, but not consistently.

Then we stopped our Gazette subscription and I found that I had much more time on my hands.

Now I sometimes try the larger NYT Games puzzle online. My skills may be rusty but I still can twig in to the puzzle maker‚Äôs thinking. It is much easier to do it now, because you don‚Äôt need to go looking for each clue; it‚Äôs immediately presented to you as you hop from word to word.

So, enjoy doing the MINI daily and use your time for other worthwhile activities!
